## SG 1

[Trivial symmetry indicator group, ℤ₁]

**~~~1<sup>st</sup>~~~ minimal solution:** νᵀ = 2 (1 symmetry vector)

| nᵀ                                         |
|:-------------------------------------------|
| [2R₁, 2T₁, 2U₁, 2V₁, 2X₁, 2Y₁, 2Z₁, (▪)²ᵀ] |

**~~~2<sup>nd</sup>~~~ minimal solution:** νᵀ = 3 (1 symmetry vector)
